\subsection{Detailed Description}
Register File containing hardware definitions and other configurations by the T\-P\-S23861 software A\-P\-I functions. \begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
January 2013
\end{DoxyDate}
This file contains the software structures, defines, and prototypes for the \hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8c}{T\-P\-S23861.\-c} A\-P\-I functions

\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_ad50108944471b1be06ae3be4239da51a}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Config\-Device4\-Pair@{tps\-\_\-\-Config\-Device4\-Pair}}
\index{tps\-\_\-\-Config\-Device4\-Pair@{tps\-\_\-\-Config\-Device4\-Pair}!TPS23861.h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Config\-Device4\-Pair}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Config\-Device4\-Pair (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-On\-\_\-\-Off\-\_\-t}}]{on\-\_\-off\-\_\-\-Port12, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Four\-\_\-\-Pair\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Mode\-Port12, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-On\-\_\-\-Off\-\_\-t}}]{on\-\_\-off\-\_\-\-Port34, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Four\-\_\-\-Pair\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Mode\-Port34}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_ad50108944471b1be06ae3be4239da51a}


Configures two ports to be used together as 4 pair operation. 

The T\-P\-S23861 allows ports 1 \& 2 or ports 3 \& 4 to operate together to perform 4 pair P\-S\-E. There a a number of different disconnect modes that can be applied to a 4-\/pair port set. This function allows the user to enable the 4-\/pair port sets and define the disconnection mode to be used.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em on\-\_\-off\-\_\-\-Port12} & Enables ports 1 \& 2 to operate in 4-\/pair mode (T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-N) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Mode\-Port12} & Disconnection mode for the 4-\/pair port set using ports 1 and 2 \mbox{[}F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D, F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-L\-O\-W\-E\-R\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T, F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-H\-I\-G\-H\-E\-R\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T, F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-E\-I\-T\-H\-E\-R\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T, or F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-B\-O\-T\-H\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T\-S\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em on\-\_\-off\-\_\-\-Port34} & Enables ports 3 \& 4 to operate in 4-\/pair mode (T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-N) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Mode\-Port34} & Disconnection mode for the 4-\/pair port set using ports 3 and 4 \mbox{[}F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D, F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-L\-O\-W\-E\-R\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T, F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-H\-I\-G\-H\-E\-R\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T, F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-E\-I\-T\-H\-E\-R\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T, or F\-O\-U\-R\-\_\-\-P\-A\-I\-R\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-B\-A\-S\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-B\-O\-T\-H\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T\-S\mbox{]}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Two\-\_\-\-Event\-\_\-t}}]{two\-Event, }

\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Disconnect\-\_\-\-Threshold\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Threshold, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-\-Config\-\_\-t}}]{icut\-Current\-Threshold, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-P\-O\-E\-\_\-\-Plus\-\_\-\-Foldback\-\_\-t}}]{poep\-Foldback\-Curve}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a2b787818ef7e374af218c952d3ca8a08}


Configures the current thresholds and operating modes for the specified port. 

The T\-P\-S23861 has a number of the threshold values and operating modes that determine the characteristic capabilities of a given port. This includes whether the port can detect class 5 devices or operate in legacy detection modes. This function allows the user to configure the characteristics for a given port.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em system\-Port\-Num} & Port Number Value returned from the port registration function, \hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8c_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port()} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em operating\-Mode} & Define the operating mode for the port \mbox{[}O\-P\-E\-R\-A\-T\-I\-N\-G\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F, O\-P\-E\-R\-A\-T\-I\-N\-G\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-M\-A\-N\-U\-A\-L, O\-P\-E\-R\-A\-T\-I\-N\-G\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-S\-E\-M\-I\-\_\-\-A\-U\-T\-O, or O\-P\-E\-R\-A\-T\-I\-N\-G\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-A\-U\-T\-O\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em legacy\-Detect} & The system can perform combinations of standard and legacy detections \mbox{[}L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\-\_\-\-D\-E\-T\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D, L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\-\_\-\-D\-E\-T\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-O\-N\-L\-Y, or L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\-\_\-\-D\-E\-T\-E\-C\-T\-\_\-\-S\-T\-A\-N\-D\-A\-R\-D\-\_\-\-T\-H\-E\-N\-\_\-\-L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em two\-Event} & The system can attempt two event physical layer classifications when a class 4 or class 5 P\-D is found \mbox{[}T\-W\-O\-\_\-\-E\-V\-E\-N\-T\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-A\-B\-L\-E, T\-W\-O\-\_\-\-E\-V\-E\-N\-T\-\_\-\-A\-F\-T\-E\-R\-\_\-\-C\-L\-A\-S\-S\-\_\-4, T\-W\-O\-\_\-\-E\-V\-E\-N\-T\-\_\-\-A\-F\-T\-E\-R\-\_\-\-C\-L\-A\-S\-S\-\_\-5, or T\-W\-O\-\_\-\-E\-V\-E\-N\-T\-\_\-\-A\-F\-T\-E\-R\-\_\-\-C\-L\-A\-S\-S\-\_\-4\-\_\-\-O\-R\-\_\-5\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em class5\-Enable} & Allows the system to attempt Class 5 current levels \mbox{[}T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-N or T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Threshold} & Current threshold for disconnection \mbox{[}D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-7\-\_\-5\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-15\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, or D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-50\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em icut\-Current\-Threshold} & I\-C\-U\-T Current threshold \mbox{[}I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-110\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-204\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-374\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-592\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-686\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-754\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, or I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-920\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em poep\-Foldback\-Curve} & Defines the foldback curve applied to a port when it is turned on \mbox{[}\-\_\-1\-X\-\_\-\-I\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-\-F\-O\-L\-D\-B\-A\-C\-K\-\_\-\-C\-U\-R\-V\-E or \-\_\-2\-X\-\_\-\-I\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-\-F\-O\-L\-D\-B\-A\-C\-K\-\_\-\-C\-U\-R\-V\-E\mbox{]}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-On\-\_\-\-Off\-\_\-t}}]{clear\-Event, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{power\-Enable\-Port\-Events, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{power\-Good\-Port\-Events, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{detection\-Port\-Events, }

\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238\-X\-\_\-\-Supply\-\_\-\-Event\-\_\-\-Register\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{supply\-Events}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a9ed3aca04ebe30dc02a02b2f8fe6ebc0}


Returns all of the individual event/fault registers that generated a T\-P\-S23861 interrupt. 

There are a number of events and faults that can generate an interrupt. This function returns the individual indicators for each of the interruptable event/fault conditions.

Calling this function will clear the interrupts associated with these events/faults, so the user should process all indicators present.

There are individual functions that return the event/fault status for an individual register.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em clear\-Event} & T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-N will cause the events to be cleared in the hardware, T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F will just read the current value of the events \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$power\-Enable\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports containing a power enable status change \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$power\-Good\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports containing a power good status change \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$detection\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports that had a detection cycle \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$classification\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports that had a classification cycle \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$icut\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports that had a I\-C\-U\-T fault \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$disconnect\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports that had a disconnect event \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$inrush\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports that had a inrush fault at port turn on \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$ilim\-Port\-Events} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports that had a I\-L\-I\-M fault occurred \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$supply\-Events} & Address of a \hyperlink{struct_t_p_s238_x___supply___event___register__t}{T\-P\-S238\-X\-\_\-\-Supply\-\_\-\-Event\-\_\-\-Register\-\_\-t} variable that will receive the supply event faults V\-P\-U\-V\-\_\-\-V\-Power\-\_\-\-Undervoltage\-\_\-\-Event V\-D\-U\-V\-\_\-\-Vdd\-\_\-\-U\-V\-L\-O\-\_\-\-Event T\-S\-D\-\_\-\-Thermal\-\_\-\-Shutdown\-\_\-\-Event\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Since the individual hardware registers contain more than one status in them, event status cannot be processed individually.
\end{DoxyNote}

\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Device\-Disconnect\-Enable}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Device\-Disconnect\-Enable (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{disconnect\-Ports}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a2d95cddf597e82edb7c11390c2d18193}


Returns the ports that are enabled for 2 pair disconnection operation. 

This function will return the ports that are configured for 2 pair disconnect operations. Disconnect operation consists of measuring the port current at the S\-E\-Nn pin, starting the T\-D\-I\-S timer when the current drops below the threshold, and turning the port off if the timer times out.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$disconnect\-Ports} & Address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that will receive the ports that are enabled for 2 pair disconnection with one bit for each port in disconnect enabled state.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}

\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Device\-Interrupt\-Status}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Device\-Interrupt\-Status (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238\-X\-\_\-\-Interrupt\-\_\-\-Register\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{status}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a7d92a16660cdfa091dc9c6983f201798}


Get the current interrupt status for the indicated T\-P\-S23861 part. 

The function returns a variable that has a one bit indicator for each of the interrupts in the T\-P\-S23861.

The interrupt mask register identifies which events/faults will generate an interrupt. The status register will still indicate events/faults that are masked and would not generate an interrupt. If the user wants to only process unmasked interrupts, the results from this function must be combined with the interrupt mask (tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Interrupt\-Mask)


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$status} & Address of a \hyperlink{struct_t_p_s238_x___interrupt___register__t}{T\-P\-S238\-X\-\_\-\-Interrupt\-\_\-\-Register\-\_\-t} variable that will receive the current interrupt status P\-E\-C\-\_\-\-Power\-\_\-\-Enable\-\_\-\-Change P\-G\-C\-\_\-\-Power\-\_\-\-Good\-\_\-\-Change D\-I\-S\-F\-\_\-\-Disconnect\-\_\-\-Event D\-E\-T\-C\-\_\-\-Detection\-\_\-\-Cycle C\-L\-A\-S\-C\-\_\-\-Classification\-\_\-\-Cycle I\-F\-A\-U\-L\-T\-\_\-\-I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-\-I\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-\-Fault I\-N\-R\-F\-\_\-\-Inrush\-\_\-\-Fault S\-U\-P\-F\-\_\-\-Supply\-\_\-\-Event\-\_\-\-Fault\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_accc2312ce106747a2e7cc9b95eef3aca}


Returns the temperature of the specified T\-P\-S23861. 

This function will return the temperature of the specified T\-P\-S23861.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$temperature} & The address of a uint8\-\_\-t variable where the temperature of the T\-P\-S23861. The temperature will be a scaled integer with an L\-S\-B of 0.\-652 degrees Celsius\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status) 
\end{DoxyReturn}

The function will return a 0 (C\-L\-A\-S\-S\-\_\-\-U\-N\-K\-N\-O\-W\-N) when the port is turned off.

The function will return a 0 (C\-L\-A\-S\-S\-\_\-\-U\-N\-K\-N\-O\-W\-N) when the port is turned off.

\hline

This function will return the detection resistance and detection status for the registered system port on a T\-P\-S23861.

\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_a1a705cbee0d106474710dcf7d0538d3a}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Detect\-Voltage\-Difference@{tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Detect\-Voltage\-Difference}}
\index{tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Detect\-Voltage\-Difference@{tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Detect\-Voltage\-Difference}!TPS23861.h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Detect\-Voltage\-Difference}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Detect\-Voltage\-Difference (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{system\-Port\-Num, }
\item[{uint16\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{detect\-Voltage\-Diff, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Detect\-\_\-\-Voltage\-\_\-\-Difference\-\_\-\-Status\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{detect\-Voltage\-Diff\-Status}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a1a705cbee0d106474710dcf7d0538d3a}


Returns the voltage difference for the indicated system port number on one of the T\-P\-S23861 in the system. 

The system will attempt to determine a legacy P\-D by measuring the P\-D input capacitance on the P\-I. A fixed charge is injected into the P\-I and the resulting voltage difference is reported. The reported voltage difference is only usable when the status indicates a valid measurement.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em system\-Port\-Num} & Port Number Value returned from the port registration function, \hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8c_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port()} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$detect\-Voltage\-Diff} & The address of a uint16\-\_\-t variable where the detection resistance of the port. The detection resistance will be a scaled integer with an L\-S\-B of 11.\-0966 ohms. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$detect\-Voltage\-Diff\-Status} & The address of a T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Detect\-\_\-\-Voltage\-\_\-\-Difference\-\_\-\-Status\-\_\-t variable for the most recent detect voltage difference result status \mbox{[}V\-D\-S\-\_\-\-S\-T\-A\-T\-U\-S\-\_\-\-P\-O\-W\-E\-R\-\_\-\-O\-N\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-E\-T, V\-D\-S\-\_\-\-S\-T\-A\-T\-U\-S\-\_\-\-V\-A\-L\-I\-D\-\_\-\-M\-E\-A\-S\-U\-R\-E\-M\-E\-N\-T, V\-D\-S\-\_\-\-S\-T\-A\-T\-U\-S\-\_\-\-T\-I\-M\-E\-O\-U\-T, V\-D\-S\-\_\-\-S\-T\-A\-T\-U\-S\-\_\-\-F\-I\-R\-S\-T\-\_\-\-M\-E\-A\-S\-U\-R\-E\-M\-E\-N\-T\-\_\-\-E\-X\-C\-E\-S\-S, V\-D\-S\-\_\-\-S\-T\-A\-T\-U\-S\-\_\-\-S\-E\-C\-O\-N\-D\-\_\-\-M\-E\-A\-S\-U\-R\-E\-M\-E\-N\-T\-\_\-\-E\-X\-C\-E\-S\-S, or V\-D\-S\-\_\-\-S\-T\-A\-T\-U\-S\-\_\-\-I\-N\-S\-U\-F\-F\-I\-C\-I\-E\-N\-T\-\_\-\-S\-I\-G\-N\-A\-L\mbox{]}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Measurements}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Get\-Port\-Measurements (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{uint16\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{voltage, }
\item[{uint16\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{current}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_aea33e295bb735809ad2edf78ed8b2543}


Returns the voltage and current of the registered system port. 

This function will return the voltage and current on the registered port on a specific T\-P\-S23861.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em system\-Port\-Num} & Port Number Value returned from the port registration function, \hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8c_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port()} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$voltage} & The address of a uint16\-\_\-t variable where the voltage of the indicated port will be placed. The voltage will be a scaled integer with an L\-S\-B of 3.\-662 m\-Volts \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em $\ast$current} & The address of a uint16\-\_\-t variable where the current of the indicated port will be placed. The current will be a scaled integer with an L\-S\-B that is dependent on the current-\/sense resistor. For a 250 m\-Ohm resistor, the L\-S\-B will be 62.\-260 micro-\/\-Amps. For a 255 m\-Ohm resistor, the L\-S\-B will be 61.\-039 micro-\/\-Amps.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}

This function can be used if the System Port Number returned in the \hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8c_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port()} function is lost or not maintained.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8h_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port} () 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port@{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port}}
\index{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port@{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port}!TPS23861.h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint16\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Port\-Num\-\_\-t}}]{device\-Port\-Num}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}


Allocates a system level port number for a given T\-P\-S23861 device and it's specific port number. 

It is easier for users to maintain a system with 4 T\-P\-S23861 with 4 ports each, when each port has a unique number. By registering each of the 16 individual ports (in this example), the user can work with ports 0-\/15, rather than have to maintain device 1 -\/ port 0, through device 4 -\/ port 3.

This function must be called prior to any function call that has a system\-Port\-Num as an input. The current logic has room for T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-M\-A\-X\-\_\-\-S\-Y\-S\-T\-E\-M\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T\-S (64) ports. The T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-Port\-Map\mbox{[}\mbox{]} variable can be modified to support more ports (or save some memory by supporting fewer).


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-Port\-Num} & T\-P\-S238\-X\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T\-\_\-1 -\/ T\-P\-S238\-X\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T\-\_\-4, The port number O\-N T\-H\-E S\-P\-E\-C\-I\-F\-I\-C T\-P\-S23861 device\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t system\-Port\-Num Unique handle that will be used to refer to this device and port number in future function calls. 

T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-P\-O\-R\-T\-\_\-\-A\-V\-A\-I\-L\-A\-B\-L\-E No port number available, all are in use
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Disconnect\-Enable}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Disconnect\-Enable (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Ports, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Disconnect\-\_\-\-Threshold\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Threshold1, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Disconnect\-\_\-\-Threshold\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Threshold2, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Disconnect\-\_\-\-Threshold\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Threshold3, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Disconnect\-\_\-\-Threshold\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Threshold4}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a8b1565bcc24973f92353ce165332f1c2}


Configures the ports to configure those that are enabled for 2 pair disconnection operation. 

This function will configure all four ports to identify which ones support disconnection operations. If the user wishes to configure a single port, the \hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8c_a7d110496e25b21006c33874d7930528d}{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Disconnect\-Enable()} is used.

Disconnect operation consists of measuring the port current at the S\-E\-Nn pin, starting the T\-D\-I\-S timer when the current drops below the threshold, and turning the port off if the timer times out.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Ports} & A T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t variable that contains the ports that will be enabled for 2 pair disconnection with one bit for each port. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Threshold1} & Disconnection threshold for port 1 \mbox{[}D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-7\-\_\-5\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-15\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P or D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-50\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Threshold2} & Disconnection threshold for port 2 \mbox{[}D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-7\-\_\-5\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-15\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P or D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-50\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Threshold3} & Disconnection threshold for port 3 \mbox{[}D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-7\-\_\-5\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-15\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P or D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-50\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Threshold4} & Disconnection threshold for port 4 \mbox{[}D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-7\-\_\-5\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-15\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P or D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-50\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P\mbox{]}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_ab4a8ca2fe81c8c8cb6764cf445015e33}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Power\-On@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Power\-On}}

\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Power\-On}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Power\-On (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Ports\-\_\-t}}]{ports\-Powered\-On}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_ab4a8ca2fe81c8c8cb6764cf445015e33}


Configures the power on state for each of the device ports on a specific T\-P\-S23861. 

This function will power on multiple ports at the same time. Each of the ports indicated in the T\-P\-S23861 will be powered on.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_ad9319af09f1461888aefa7d1439986a2}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Timing@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Timing}}
\index{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Timing@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Timing}!TPS23861.h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Timing}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Device\-Timing (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-I\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-\-Timing\-\_\-t}}]{ilim\-Timing, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-T\-Start\-\_\-\-Timing\-\_\-t}}]{start\-Timing, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-T\-I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-\-Timing\-\_\-t}}]{icut\-Timing, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-T\-D\-I\-S\-\_\-\-Timing\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Timing, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Cool\-\_\-\-Down\-\_\-\-Timing\-\_\-t}}]{cool\-Down\-Fault\-Timing}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_ad9319af09f1461888aefa7d1439986a2}


Configures the timing of the various current limits and disconnection determinations for a given device in the system. 

The T\-P\-S23861 has three levels of overcurrent protections, disconnection detection, and time out after fault conditions. In order to prevent glitches or transients from causing unnecessary shutdowns or faults, the system uses various timers to define the amount of time required over the threshold level before a fault or shutdown is declared.

This function sets up the various timing parameters used in the system. These timings are applicable on all active ports.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em device\-\_\-i2c\-\_\-address} & 7 bit I2\-C address of the T\-P\-S238x part being controlled (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ilim\-Timing} & The I\-L\-I\-M Fault Timing which is the foldback current time limit before port turn off \mbox{[}T\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-60\-\_\-\-M\-S, T\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-S, T\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-15\-\_\-\-M\-S, or T\-L\-I\-M\-\_\-10\-\_\-\-M\-S\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em start\-Timing} & The length of the T\-S\-T\-A\-R\-T period, which is the maximum amount of allowed overcurrent time during inrush \mbox{[}T\-S\-T\-A\-R\-T\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-S, T\-S\-T\-A\-R\-T\-\_\-60\-\_\-\-M\-S, or T\-S\-T\-A\-R\-T\-\_\-120\-\_\-\-M\-S\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em icut\-Timing} & I\-C\-U\-T Fault timing, which is the overcurrent time duration before port turn off \mbox{[}T\-I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-S, T\-I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-60\-\_\-\-M\-S, T\-I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-120\-\_\-\-M\-S, or T\-I\-C\-U\-T\-\_\-240\-\_\-\-M\-S\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Timing} & Disconnect delay, which is the time to turn off a port once there is a disconnect condition \mbox{[}T\-D\-I\-S\-\_\-90\-\_\-\-M\-S, T\-D\-I\-S\-\_\-180\-\_\-\-M\-S, T\-D\-I\-S\-\_\-360\-\_\-\-M\-S, or T\-D\-I\-S\-\_\-720\-\_\-\-M\-S\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em cool\-Down\-Fault\-Timing} & Amount of time before a port can turn back on after fault \mbox{[}C\-O\-O\-L\-\_\-\-D\-O\-W\-N\-\_\-1\-\_\-\-S\-E\-C, C\-O\-O\-L\-\_\-\-D\-O\-W\-N\-\_\-2\-\_\-\-S\-E\-C, or C\-O\-O\-L\-\_\-\-D\-O\-W\-N\-\_\-4\-\_\-\-S\-E\-C\mbox{]}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}

\hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8h_ad50108944471b1be06ae3be4239da51a}{tps\-\_\-\-Config\-Device4\-Pair} () 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_a0039fc214b60c4d3c249b33453cf6065}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Set\-I2\-C\-Addresses@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-I2\-C\-Addresses}}
\index{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-I2\-C\-Addresses@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-I2\-C\-Addresses}!TPS23861.h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-I2\-C\-Addresses}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Set\-I2\-C\-Addresses (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{temp\-\_\-i2c\-Address, }
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{num\-Devices, }
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{list\-\_\-of\-Addresses, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-On\-\_\-\-Off\-\_\-t} $\ast$}]{list\-\_\-of\-Auto\-Mode}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a0039fc214b60c4d3c249b33453cf6065}


Allows a set of T\-P\-S23861 to be configured with unique I2\-C addresses. 

The system is designed so a number of T\-P\-S23861 can be placed on the same I2\-C bus. For this to work, each device must have a unique I2\-C address to allow them to be individually commanded. This function will program a set of T\-P\-S23861 devices on the same I2\-C bus with different addresses. The new I2\-C address will be stored in non-\/volatile memory and become the new I2\-C address for the specific part, even after power off.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em temp\-\_\-i2c\-Address} & A temporary 7 bit I2\-C address that will be used during the address programming of the T\-P\-S238x parts (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em num\-Devices} & Number of T\-P\-S23861 devices on the I2\-C bus \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em list\-\_\-of\-Addresses} & A pointer to a list of uint8\-\_\-t 7 bit I2\-C addresses for each of the T\-P\-S23861 parts on the I2\-C bus (do not included R/\-W bit) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em list\-\_\-of\-Auto\-Mode} & A pointer to a list of T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-On\-\_\-\-Off\-\_\-t values that contain T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-N for the devices that operate in A\-U\-T\-O mode and T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F for those that do not operate in A\-U\-T\-O mode\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_a60e64452aad48caf62d2e2e590471666}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Detect\-Class\-Enable@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Detect\-Class\-Enable}}

\hypertarget{_t_p_s23861_8h_a7d110496e25b21006c33874d7930528d}{\index{T\-P\-S23861.\-h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}!tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Disconnect\-Enable@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Disconnect\-Enable}}
\index{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Disconnect\-Enable@{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Disconnect\-Enable}!TPS23861.h@{T\-P\-S23861.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Disconnect\-Enable}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint8\-\_\-t tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Port\-Disconnect\-Enable (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\-\_\-t}]{system\-Port\-Num, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-On\-\_\-\-Off\-\_\-t}}]{on\-\_\-off, }
\item[{{\bf T\-P\-S238x\-\_\-\-Disconnect\-\_\-\-Threshold\-\_\-t}}]{disconnect\-Threshold}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{_t_p_s23861_8h_a7d110496e25b21006c33874d7930528d}


Configures a single port to enable or disable the 2 pair disconnection operation. 

This function will configure one of the four ports to enable or disable disconnection operations. If the user wishes to configure a all ports at once, the tps\-\_\-\-Set\-Disconnect\-Enable() is used.

Disconnect operation consists of measuring the port current at the S\-E\-Nn pin, starting the T\-D\-I\-S timer when the current drops below the threshold, and turning the port off if the timer times out.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em system\-Port\-Num} & Port Number Value returned from the port registration function, \hyperlink{_t_p_s23861_8c_a915cc811128c70c54ff0ac048cfbc6e7}{tps\-\_\-\-Register\-Port()} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em on\-\_\-off} & T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-N to enable disconnection operations for the indicated port, T\-P\-S\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F otherwise \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em disconnect\-Threshold} & Disconnection threshold for indicated port \mbox{[}D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-7\-\_\-5\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-15\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P, D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-30\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P or D\-C\-T\-H\-\_\-50\-\_\-\-M\-I\-L\-L\-I\-A\-M\-P\mbox{]}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint8\-\_\-t (I2\-C\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S\-F\-U\-L or I2\-C error status)
\end{DoxyReturn}
